  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:right;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;">Exhibit 99.1</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><img src="img125957890_0.jpg" alt="img125957890_0.jpg" style="width:213px;height:87px;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;">	</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Terns Pharmaceuticals Reports Second Quarter 2021 Financial Results and Corporate Highlights</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">-Top-line data from ongoing Phase 1 proof of concept clinical trial of TERN-501 expected in 4Q 2021</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">-Top-line data readout from Part 1 of ongoing AVIATION Trial of TERN-201 expected in 1H 2022</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">-Cash and equivalents of $185.1 million provides runway into 2024</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">FOSTER CITY, Calif., August 16, 2021 &#x2013; Terns Pharmaceuticals, Inc. (&#x201c;Terns&#x201d; or the &#x201c;Company&#x201d;) (Nasdaq: TERN), a clinical-stage biopharmaceutical company developing a portfolio of small-molecule single-agent and combination therapy candidates for the treatment of non-alcoholic steatohepatitis (NASH) and other chronic liver diseases, today reported financial results for the second quarter ended June 30, 2021 and corporate highlights.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;"> </font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">&#x201c;We are pleased to report significant progress across our clinical programs this quarter marked by several important achievements, including initiations of our Phase 1b AVIATION Trial of TERN-201 and the multiple ascending dose (MAD) cohort of our TERN-501 Phase 1 trial, as well as positive top-line data from our Phase 2a LIFT Study of TERN-101,&#x201d; said Senthil Sundaram, Chief Executive Officer at Terns. &#x201c;These milestones highlight our commitment to rapidly advance our broad NASH pipeline. We look forward to proof of concept data for TERN-501 later this year and for TERN-201 in 2022.&#x201d;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Recent Developments and Anticipated Upcoming Milestones</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">TERN-501: Thyroid hormone receptor-beta (THR-&#x3b2;) agonist</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:4.533%;display:flex;margin-top:6.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;display:inline-block;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;">&#xf0b7;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Initiated 14-day multiple ascending dose (MAD) portion of Phase 1 trial in June 2021</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:4.533%;display:flex;margin-top:6.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;display:inline-block;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;">&#xf0b7;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Top-line, proof of concept data readout expected in 4Q 2021, including:</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:9.067%;display:flex;margin-top:6.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;display:inline-block;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;">o</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Pharmacodynamic markers of THR-&#x3b2; engagement in the liver linked to NASH efficacy, including sex hormone binding globulin (SHBG) and low-density lipoprotein (LDL) cholesterol</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:9.067%;display:flex;margin-top:6.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;display:inline-block;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;">o</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Indicators of pharmacokinetic stability</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:9.067%;display:flex;margin-top:6.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;display:inline-block;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;">o</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Safety and tolerability</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">&#160;</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:4.533%;display:flex;margin-top:6.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;display:inline-block;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;">&#xf0b7;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Received Fast Track Designation (FTD) from the U.S. FDA in June 2021</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:9.067%;display:flex;margin-top:6.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;display:inline-block;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;">o</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Provides eligibility for more frequent FDA interactions, accelerated approval and priority review</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:9.067%;display:flex;margin-top:6.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;display:inline-block;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;">o</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">TERN-501 is Terns&#x2019; third development-stage compound with FTD for the treatment of NASH</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">&#160;</font></p>

  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;">&#160;</font></p>

  <div style="margin-left:4.533%;display:flex;margin-top:6.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;display:inline-block;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;">&#xf0b7;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Initiated 12-week Phase 1b AVIATION Trial in NASH in June 2021</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:4.533%;display:flex;margin-top:6.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;display:inline-block;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;">&#xf0b7;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Top-line results from Part 1 of AVIATION Trial expected in 1H 2022, including:</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:9.067%;display:flex;margin-top:6.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;display:inline-block;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;">o</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Key efficacy readout in corrected T1 (cT1), an imaging marker of liver inflammation and fibrosis linked to clinical outcomes</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:9.067%;display:flex;margin-top:6.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;display:inline-block;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;">o</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Safety, tolerability and plasma VAP-1 activity</font></div></div>

  <div style="margin-left:9.067%;display:flex;margin-top:6.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;display:inline-block;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;">o</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">First FXR agonist trial to demonstrate no discontinuations due to adverse events, including pruritus </font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:9.067%;display:flex;margin-top:6.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;display:inline-block;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;">o</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">First 12-week placebo-controlled trial of an FXR agonist in NASH to show significant improvements in cT1, an imaging marker of liver inflammation and fibrosis linked to clinical outcomes</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:9.067%;display:flex;margin-top:6.0pt;line-height:1.3;justify-content:flex-start;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;display:inline-block;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Symbol;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:0.3402777777777778in;">o</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">First FXR agonist planned to be studied in combination with a THR-&#x3b2; agonist (TERN-501)</font></div></div>

  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.4950000000000003;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;">&#160;</font></p>
  <hr style="page-break-after:always;">
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="font-size:12.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">About Terns Pharmaceuticals</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Terns Pharmaceuticals, Inc. is a clinical-stage biopharmaceutical company developing a portfolio of small-molecule single-agent and combination therapy candidates for the treatment of non-alcoholic steatohepatitis, or NASH, and other chronic liver diseases. Terns&#x2019; pipeline includes three clinical stage development programs including an FXR agonist, a VAP-1 inhibitor and a THR-&#x3b2; agonist, and a preclinical GLP-1 receptor agonist program. Terns is focused on developing combination therapies based on clinically validated and complementary mechanisms of action to address the multiple hepatic disease processes of NASH in order to drive meaningful clinical benefits for patients. For more information, please visit: </font><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;text-decoration:underline;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">www.ternspharma.com</font><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">.</font><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;"> </font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Calibri;">Cautionary Note Regarding Forward-Looking Statements</font></p>
